   1: // I-p2-029 (#768): single source of truth for the primary nav.
   2: // Consumed by BOTH AppShell and HomeKeyboardShell so the nav can never drift
   3: // between shells (previously the PRIMARY_NAV const was duplicated in each).
   4: 
   5: import type { RoleId } from "@/lib/roles";
   6: 
   7: export interface NavItem {
   8:   href: string;
   9:   label: string;
  10:   /** Roles that may SEE this item (presentation-only — not authorization).
  11:    * Omitted = visible to all roles. */
  12:   roles?: readonly RoleId[];
  13: }
  14: 
  15: export const PRIMARY_NAV: readonly NavItem[] = [
  16:   { href: "/", label: "Home" },
  17:   { href: "/intake", label: "Intake" },
  18:   { href: "/dashboard", label: "Dashboard" },
  19:   { href: "/upload", label: "Upload" },
  20:   { href: "/benchmark", label: "Benchmark" },
  21:   { href: "/compare", label: "Compare" },
  22:   { href: "/contracts", label: "Contracts" },
  23:   { href: "/pin_replay", label: "Pin Replay" },
  24:   { href: "/memory", label: "Memory" },
  25: ];
  26: 
  27: /** Presentation-only nav filter by role. Pure + isomorphic (safe in server or
  28:  * client). Items without a `roles` list are visible to every role. */
  29: export function navForRole(
  30:   items: readonly NavItem[],
  31:   role: RoleId,
  32: ): readonly NavItem[] {
  33:   return items.filter((item) => !item.roles || item.roles.includes(role));
  34: }

   1: // I-cd-022 (#612): pathname-aware AppShell gate. On `/`, suppress BOTH
   2: // the AppShell header AND its <main> wrapper so the home route can
   3: // provide its own header (with the same primary nav) + its own <main>.
   4: // This avoids G1 (double header) + G6 (nested main) landmark violations.
   5: //
   6: // Tiny "use client" boundary so the otherwise server-rendered AppShell
   7: // can still wrap every non-home route on the server.
   8: "use client";
   9: 
  10: import { usePathname } from "next/navigation";
  11: 
  12: import { AppShell } from "@/components/app_shell";
  13: 
  14: interface AppShellGateProps {
  15:   children: React.ReactNode;
  16: }
  17: 
  18: export function AppShellGate({ children }: AppShellGateProps) {
  19:   const pathname = usePathname();
  20:   // Home owns its own header + main; render children bare on `/`.
  21:   if (pathname === "/") {
  22:     return <>{children}</>;
  23:   }
  24:   return <AppShell>{children}</AppShell>;
  25: }

   7:  * I-cd-004: client component for top-nav active-route highlight. Pure styling
   8:  * via the locked shadcn token set (accent / muted-foreground / foreground).
   9:  * Active when the pathname equals href, or starts with `${href}/` for nested
  10:  * routes (e.g. `/runs/abc` highlights "Dashboard" only if we want — by default
  11:  * an item is active for its own subtree).
  12:  */
  13: export function NavLink({
  14:   href,
  15:   children,
  16: }: {
  17:   href: string;
  18:   children: React.ReactNode;
  19: }) {
  20:   const pathname = usePathname();
  21:   const is_active =
  22:     pathname === href || (href !== "/" && pathname.startsWith(`${href}/`));
  23:   return (
  24:     <Link
  25:       href={href}
  26:       aria-current={is_active ? "page" : undefined}
  27:       className={
  28:         "rounded-md px-3 py-1.5 text-sm font-medium transition-colors " +
  29:         (is_active
  30:           ? "bg-accent text-accent-foreground"
  31:           : "text-muted-foreground hover:bg-accent/50 hover:text-foreground")
  32:       }
  33:     >
  34:       {children}
  35:     </Link>
  36:   );
  37: }
